            // ensures js doesn't die if ads service fails.  
            // Note that we need to define the js here, since ad js is being rendered inline after this.
            (function(f) {
                // Fallback javascript, when the ad Service call fails.  
                
                if((window.csm == null || window.generic == null || window.consoleLog == null)) {
                    if (window.console && console.log) {
                        console.log("one or more of window.csm, window.generic or window.consoleLog has been stubbed...");
                    }
                }

            <div class="inline">
    Nicolas Cage was born Nicolas Kim Coppola in Long Beach, California, the son of comparative literature professor <a href="/name/nm1692024?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk1">August Coppola</a> (whose brother is director <a href="/name/nm0000338?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk2">Francis Ford Coppola</a>) and dancer/choreographer Joy Vogelsang. He is of Italian (father) and Polish, German, and English (mother) descent. Cage changed his name early in his career to make his ...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">

>See full bio</a> &raquo;
            </span>
</div>        </div>

    (1998, Movieline Magazine) I see <a href="/name/nm0002537?ref_=nm_dyk_qt1">Miles Davis</a> as a surrealist father of mine. He was the first person to believe in me as an actor, the one who first said he understood what I was talking about. It was on <a href="/title/tt0063894?ref_=nm_dyk_qt2">The Dick Cavett Show</a> (1968). Before we went on he said to me, "Why aren't you wearing your leather jacket? Didn't you learn anything from <a href="/name/nm0000454?ref_=nm_dyk_qt3">Dennis Hopper</a>?" Because I was wearing a suit. Then I went...                    <span class="see-more inline">
